--cpu_clk is cpu_clk and unplaced

--operation mode is input

cpu_clk = INPUT();

--cpu_rst is cpu_rst and unplaced

--operation mode is input

cpu_rst = INPUT();

--A1L2 is cpu_clk~clkctrl and unplaced

A1L2 = cycloneii_clkctrl(.INCLK[0] = cpu_clk) WITH (clock_type = "Global Clock");

--A1L21 is cpu_rst~clkctrl and unplaced

A1L21 = cycloneii_clkctrl(.INCLK[0] = cpu_rst) WITH (clock_type = "Global Clock");

--E1L5 is ctrl_unit:Unit0|controller:U0|IRld_ctrl~clkctrl and unplaced

E1L5 = cycloneii_clkctrl(.INCLK[0] = E1_IRld_ctrl) WITH (clock_type = "Global Clock");
